     </span>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         success\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         1 day, 23 hours, 12 minutes\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         60%\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39">\n          <a href="#cite_note-39">\n           [29]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mission_timeline">\n        Mission timeline\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Mission timeline">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="15_July_(Flight_Day_1,_Launch)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="15_July_.28Flight_Day_1.2C_Launch.29">\n        15 July (Flight Day 1, Launch)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 15 July (Flight Day 1, Launch)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-127_Launch_05.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1996" data-file-width="3000" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/STS-127_Launch_05.jpg/220px-STS-127_Launch_05.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/STS-127_Launch_05.jpg/330px-STS-127_Launch_05.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f1/STS-127_Launch_05.jpg/440px-STS-127_Launch_05.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-127_Launch_05.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Liftoff of space shuttle Endeavour from Launch Pad 39A\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On 15 July 2009 at 18:03:10 EDT, the launch was finally successful.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40">\n        <a href="#cite_note-40">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Upon reviewing the launch video footage, imagery analysts noted eight or nine instances of foam shedding from the External Tank.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41">\n        <a href="#cite_note-41">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The pictures of the external tank taken when jettisoning showed loss of foam in the intertank ribbing.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">\n        <a href="#cite_note-42">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The chairman of the Mission Management Team was not concerned and felt that the Space Shuttle would be cleared for re-entry on its return voyage\xe2\x80\x94which it was a few days later.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43">\n        <a href="#cite_note-43">\n         [33]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44">\n        <a href="#cite_note-44">\n         [34]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-45">\n        <a href="#cite_note-45">\n         [NASA 11]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The payload doors were opened after reaching orbit followed by deployment of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Ku_band" title="Ku band">\n        K\n        <sub>\n         u\n        </sub>\n        band\n       </a>\n       antenna and activation of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Canadarm" title="Canadarm">\n        shuttle\'s mechanical arm\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd2_inspections_46-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd2_inspections-46">\n         [35]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="16_July_(Flight_Day_2)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="16_July_.28Flight_Day_2.29">\n        16 July (Flight Day 2)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 16 July (Flight Day 2)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Astronaut_Julie_Payette_looks_through_an_overhead_window_on_Space_Shuttle_Endeavour.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/Astronaut_Julie_Payette_looks_through_an_overhead_window_on_Space_Shuttle_Endeavour.jpg/220px-Astronaut_Julie_Payette_looks_through_an_overhead_window_on_Space_Shuttle_Endeavour.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/Astronaut_Julie_Payette_looks_through_an_overhead_window_on_Space_Shuttle_Endeavour.jpg/330px-Astronaut_Julie_Payette_looks_through_an_overhead_window_on_Space_Shuttle_Endeavour.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/Astronaut_Julie_Payette_looks_through_an_overhead_window_on_Space_Shuttle_Endeavour.jpg/440px-Astronaut_Julie_Payette_looks_through_an_overhead_window_on_Space_Shuttle_Endeavour.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Astronaut_Julie_Payette_looks_through_an_overhead_window_on_Space_Shuttle_Endeavour.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Julie Payette looks through an overhead window while operating controls on the\n         <a href="/wiki/Aft" title="Aft">\n          aft\n         </a>\n         <a href="/wiki/Flight_deck" title="Flight deck">\n          flight deck\n         </a>\n         of Endeavour during flight day two activities.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The thermal protection system was inspected with the Shuttle Robotic Arm/Orbiter Boom Sensor System (\n       <a href="/wiki/Orbiter_Boom_Sensor_System" title="Orbiter Boom Sensor System">\n        OBSS\n       </a>\n       ) and the voluminous data downlinked for analysis. The orbital maneuvering system pods were inspected for tile damage or protruding tiles. The extravehicular mobility units were checked in addition to the rendezvous system tests and centerline camera installation. In preparation for the docking, the docking ring was extended.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd2_inspections_46-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd2_inspections-46">\n         [35]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47">\n        <a href="#cite_note-47">\n         [NASA 12]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="17_July_(Flight_Day_3,_ISS_Docking)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="17_July_.28Flight_Day_3.2C_ISS_Docking.29">\n        17 July (Flight Day 3, ISS Docking)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 17 July (Flight Day 3, ISS Docking)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The shuttle successfully docked with the station 220 miles (350\xc2\xa0km) above the Earth, following rendezvous pitch maneuver (RPM) photography of Endeavour\xe2\x80\x99s thermal protection system by the Expedition 20 Crew.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-48">\n        <a href="#cite_note-48">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       During this procedure, the shuttle flips over on its back to the station so that the station crew can capture high resolution imagery of the underside of the shuttle. The docking happened on the ISS\xe2\x80\x99s PMA-2 (Pressurized Mating Adapter) on the Harmony module and the hatch was opened after leak checks. As part of the crew swap, station crew member Koichi Wakata was replaced with Tim Kopra. The two astronauts specially fitted seatliners were interchanged.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49">\n        <a href="#cite_note-49">\n         [NASA 13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As part of preparation for EVA 1, astronauts Wolf and Kopra camped out in the Quest airlock. A quick review of the RPM imagery showed no serious concerns beyond two instances of coating loss. Further analysis of the imagery will be done. A boost of the station was completed with the shuttle\'s vernier thrusters to avoid a piece of space debris. The SRBs were retrieved and their camera imagery is expected to give more detail on the ET foam shedding.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sts127heatshield_15-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sts127heatshield-15">\n         [13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:ISS_from_Endeavour_before_docking.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/ISS_from_Endeavour_before_docking.jpg/120px-ISS_from_Endeavour_before_docking.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/ISS_from_Endeavour_before_docking.jpg/180px-ISS_from_Endeavour_before_docking.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/ISS_from_Endeavour_before_docking.jpg/240px-ISS_from_Endeavour_before_docking.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           One of Endeavour\'s aft flight deck windows frames the nearby International Space Station.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Range_finding_from_shuttle_to_ISS.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2849" data-file-width="4288" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ea/Range_finding_from_shuttle_to_ISS.jpg/120px-Range_finding_from_shuttle_to_ISS.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ea/Range_finding_from_shuttle_to_ISS.jpg/180px-Range_finding_from_shuttle_to_ISS.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ea/Range_finding_from_shuttle_to_ISS.jpg/240px-Range_finding_from_shuttle_to_ISS.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Astronaut Christopher Cassidy uses a rangefinder to determine the distance to ISS before docking\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:RPM_image_of_Endeavour.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2849" data-file-width="4288" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/RPM_image_of_Endeavour.jpg/120px-RPM_image_of_Endeavour.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/RPM_image_of_Endeavour.jpg/180px-RPM_image_of_Endeavour.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/RPM_image_of_Endeavour.jpg/240px-RPM_image_of_Endeavour.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           RPM image of Endeavour as taken from ISS\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="18_July_(Flight_Day_4,_EVA_1)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="18_July_.28Flight_Day_4.2C_EVA_1.29">\n        18 July (Flight Day 4, EVA 1)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 18 July (Flight Day 4, EVA 1)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       EVA 1 started with astronauts Dave Wolf and Tim Kopra switching their spacesuit power to internal battery at 16:19 UTC. Despite a communication problem with the spacewalkers, the Japanese Exposed Facility was successfully installed on the Japanese Experiment Module by means of a complex series of steps involving the robotic arms of both the station and the shuttle.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd4_activities1_50-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd4_activities1-50">\n         [NASA 14]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The JEF was first unberthed from the shuttle payload bay by the station arm, after which the shuttle arm took the load. The station arm was then moved to the worksite on Node-2 (Harmony), wherefrom it took the 4.1 ton facility back. The facility was then successfully latched on to the Experiment Module.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd4_activities2_51-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd4_activities2-51">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-52">\n        <a href="#cite_note-52">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-53">\n        <a href="#cite_note-53">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As part of the EVA, the spacewalkers successfully deployed the port Unpressurized Cargo Carrier Attach System (UCCAS), which could not be deployed during\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-119" title="STS-119">\n        STS-119\n       </a>\n       . During the prior mission, the deployment failed due to a jamming caused by a stuck detent pin. Engineers designed a custom tool to force the pin to release, which was used to deploy the mechanism.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd4_activities3_54-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd4_activities3-54">\n         [40]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Meanwhile, the shuttle managers announced that there would be no need for a focused inspection of the heat shield. The nose cap and wing leading-edge panels of the shuttle were cleared for entry as they were, but a reentry clearance was not given.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd4_activities1_50-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd4_activities1-50">\n         [NASA 14]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Beyond one impact site having a gouge, the rest of the impacts were found to be mostly a loss of coating.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55">\n        <a href="#cite_note-55">\n         [41]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The other activity scheduled for EVA 1, the deployment of a starboard side cargo carrier, was postponed for want of time.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd4_activities3_54-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd4_activities3-54">\n         [40]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A fuel cell issue found before launch was analyzed, though the cell continued to function as expected with no impact to the mission.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd4_activities2_51-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd4_activities2-51">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-127_EVA1_Kopra04.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/STS-127_EVA1_Kopra04.jpg/120px-STS-127_EVA1_Kopra04.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/STS-127_EVA1_Kopra04.jpg/180px-STS-127_EVA1_Kopra04.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/STS-127_EVA1_Kopra04.jpg/240px-STS-127_EVA1_Kopra04.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Tim Kopra working to prepare the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Berthing" title="Berthing">\n            berthing\n           </a>\n           mechanisms on the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kibo_laboratory" title="Kibo laboratory">\n            Kibo laboratory\n           </a>\n           and the Japanese Exposed Facility (JEF) for the JEF installation on Kibo, during space walk 1.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-127_JEM-EF.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2847" data-file-width="4288" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/06/STS-127_JEM-EF.jpg/120px-STS-127_JEM-EF.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/06/STS-127_JEM-EF.jpg/180px-STS-127_JEM-EF.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/06/STS-127_JEM-EF.jpg/240px-STS-127_JEM-EF.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           JEF in the grasp of the shuttle\'s robotic arm.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="19_July_(Flight_Day_5)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="19_July_.28Flight_Day_5.29">\n        19 July (Flight Day 5)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 19 July (Flight Day 5)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-127_ICC.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/STS-127_ICC.jpg/220px-STS-127_ICC.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/STS-127_ICC.jpg/330px-STS-127_ICC.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/STS-127_ICC.jpg/440px-STS-127_ICC.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-127_ICC.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         ICC handoff by shuttle\'s robotic arm\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The installation of the Integrated Cargo Carrier-Vertical Light Deployable (ICC-VLD) on the port side of the station was successfully completed with the use of both the shuttle and station robotic arms. The cargo pallet, containing spares and fresh batteries for the station, was lifted out of the shuttle bay by the shuttle arm and handed off to the station\'s Canadarm2, which maneuvered it to its position. The pallet\'s contents will be set up in upcoming EVAs. A malfunction in a new toilet in the Destiny laboratory caused the crew to use the one in the Russian segment while attempts were made to identify the fault. Meanwhile, the shuttle was cleared for reentry.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd5_activities1_56-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd5_activities1-56">\n         [NASA 15]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd5_activities2_57-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd5_activities2-57">\n         [42]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd5_activities3_58-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd5_activities3-58">\n         [43]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd5_toiletissue_59-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd5_toiletissue-59">\n         [44]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="20_July_(Flight_Day_6,_EVA_2)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="20_July_.28Flight_Day_6.2C_EVA_2.29">\n        20 July (Flight Day 6, EVA 2)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 20 July (Flight Day 6, EVA 2)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Astronauts Wolf and Marshburn began EVA 2 at 15:27 UTC out of the Quest airlock. The EVA was to transfer the spare components brought by the shuttle from the ICC-VLD to\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/External_Stowage_Platform" title="External Stowage Platform">\n        External Stowage Platform\n       </a>\n       -3. The spares were handled by Wolf riding the station\'s robotic arm to the P3 truss stowage platform where he and Marshburn attached them for long term storage. The purpose of the spares was to provide redundancy to the station in the period following the shuttle\'s retirement. The spares unloaded include a Ku-Band Space-to-Ground antenna, a pump module for the coolant system and a drive unit for the station\'s robotic arm\'s mobile transporter. A planned installation of a camera on the Japanese Experiment Facility was postponed to a future EVA for want of time. Meanwhile, the malfunctioning toilet was set right with the replacement of internal parts and cleared for normal use after tests.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd6_activities1_60-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd6_activities1-60">\n         [NASA 16]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd6_activities2_61-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd6_activities2-61">\n         [45]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd6_activities3_62-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd6_activities3-62">\n         [46]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd6_toilet_63-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd6_toilet-63">\n         [47]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-127_EVA2_Wolf4.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/STS-127_EVA2_Wolf4.jpg/120px-STS-127_EVA2_Wolf4.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/STS-127_EVA2_Wolf4.jpg/180px-STS-127_EVA2_Wolf4.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/STS-127_EVA2_Wolf4.jpg/240px-STS-127_EVA2_Wolf4.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Dave Wolf performs his second space walk, which is also the second of five scheduled space walks for STS-127.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Astronaut_Tom_Marshburn_performs_his_first_spacewalk.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Astronaut_Tom_Marshburn_performs_his_first_spacewalk.jpg/120px-Astronaut_Tom_Marshburn_performs_his_first_spacewalk.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Astronaut_Tom_Marshburn_performs_his_first_spacewalk.jpg/180px-Astronaut_Tom_Marshburn_performs_his_first_spacewalk.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Astronaut_Tom_Marshburn_performs_his_first_spacewalk.jpg/240px-Astronaut_Tom_Marshburn_performs_his_first_spacewalk.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Tom Marshburn performs his first space walk, the STS-127 crew\'s second of the five scheduled.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Astronaut_Tom_Marshburn_performs_his_first_spacewalk_(2).jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/Astronaut_Tom_Marshburn_performs_his_first_spacewalk_%282%29.jpg/120px-Astronaut_Tom_Marshburn_performs_his_first_spacewalk_%282%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/Astronaut_Tom_Marshburn_performs_his_first_spacewalk_%282%29.jpg/180px-Astronaut_Tom_Marshburn_performs_his_first_spacewalk_%282%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/Astronaut_Tom_Marshburn_performs_his_first_spacewalk_%282%29.jpg/240px-Astronaut_Tom_Marshburn_performs_his_first_spacewalk_%282%29.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Another view of Marshburn during his first space walk.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="21_July_(Flight_Day_7)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="21_July_.28Flight_Day_7.29">\n        21 July (Flight Day 7)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 21 July (Flight Day 7)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-127_JLE_handover.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/STS-127_JLE_handover.jpg/220px-STS-127_JLE_handover.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/STS-127_JLE_handover.jpg/330px-STS-127_JLE_handover.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/STS-127_JLE_handover.jpg/440px-STS-127_JLE_handover.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-127_JLE_handover.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Japanese logistics carrier(JLE) handoff from shuttle to station.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       In one of the more relaxed days, the Japanese logistics carrier was attached to the Japanese Exposed Facility. The cargo pallet was unberthed from the shuttle by the shuttle\'s robotic arm and handed to the station\'s robotic arm which then soft fixed it temporarily to the facility. After the experiments, containing an X-ray astronomy payload, a space environment monitor and a communications system, are installed the pallet will be returned to Earth by the shuttle.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd7_activities1_64-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd7_activities1-64">\n         [NASA 17]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd7_activities_65-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd7_activities-65">\n         [48]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="22_July_(Flight_Day_8,_EVA_3)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="22_July_.28Flight_Day_8.2C_EVA_3.29">\n        22 July (Flight Day 8, EVA 3)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: 22 July (Flight Day 8, EVA 3)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Astronaut_Christopher_Cassidy_during_STS-127%27s_third_space_walk.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Astronaut_Christopher_Cassidy_during_STS-127%27s_third_space_walk.jpg/220px-Astronaut_Christopher_Cassidy_during_STS-127%27s_third_space_walk.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Astronaut_Christopher_Cassidy_during_STS-127%27s_third_space_walk.jpg/330px-Astronaut_Christopher_Cassidy_during_STS-127%27s_third_space_walk.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Astronaut_Christopher_Cassidy_during_STS-127%27s_third_space_walk.jpg/440px-Astronaut_Christopher_Cassidy_during_STS-127%27s_third_space_walk.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Astronaut_Christopher_Cassidy_during_STS-127%27s_third_space_walk.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Cassidy works near the JEF during space walk 3.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The spacewalk involving astronauts Wolf and Cassidy started at 14:32 UTC. As part of preparation for experiment installation on the Japanese external science deck, Cassidy removed the thermal covers off the experiment carrier. Meanwhile, Wolf removed obstructions, consisting of a handrail and an equipment installation socket, from the Harmony node to clear the way for an upcoming Japanese automated resupply ship. The other task for EVA 3, involving replacement of four of the six batteries in the P6 truss, did not go as planned. Each 375 pound battery was to be removed and placed in a temporary stowage platform while a new one is taken from the ICC-VLD and fixed. The old ones will be returned to Earth. When two new batteries had been installed and three old ones removed, the CO\n       <sub>\n        2\n       </sub>\n       levels in Cassidy\'s suit showed an upward trend. Even though it never exceeded the safety limits, the EVA was called off with both astronauts returning into the station. This left one old battery in a temporary flexible stowage position. The rest of the batteries will be installed in a future EVA with the rest of the EVAs being under replanning.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd8_activities1_66-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd8_activities1-66">\n         [NASA 18]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd8_activities2_67-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd8_activities2-67">\n         [49]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd8_activities3_68-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd8_activities3-68">\n         [50]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd8_activities4_69-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd8_activities4-69">\n         [51]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="23_July_(Flight_Day_9)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="23_July_.28Flight_Day_9.29">\n        23 July (Flight Day 9)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: 23 July (Flight Day 9)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The Kibo robotic arm was inaugurated operationally with it being used to install experiments on to the Japanese exposed facility. The three experiments, transferred from the Japanese cargo pallet, consisted of\n       <a href="/wiki/MAXI_(ISS_Experiment)" title="MAXI (ISS Experiment)">\n        Monitor of All-sky X-ray Image\n       </a>\n       , Inter-orbit Communication System and Space Environment Data Acquisition Equipment-Attached Payload. As per the revised plan for EVA 4 astronauts Cassidy and Marshburn will replace the remaining four batteries on P6 and complete the already deferred installation of a camera on the Japanese experiment facility.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd9_activities1_70-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd9_activities1-70">\n         [NASA 19]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd9_activities2_71-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd9_activities2-71">\n         [NASA 20]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd9_activities3_72-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd9_activities3-72">\n         [52]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="24_July_(Flight_Day_10,_EVA_4)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="24_July_.28Flight_Day_10.2C_EVA_4.29">\n        24 July (Flight Day 10, EVA 4)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: 24 July (Flight Day 10, EVA 4)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The fourth spacewalk, by Cassidy and Marshburn, involved replacement of the final four of the six batteries on P6 truss integrated electronics assembly. After berthing the old batteries in the ICC-VLD, the cargo pallet was returned to the Endeavour\xe2\x80\x99s payload bay by the shuttle\'s robotic arm. The elevated levels of CO\n       <sub>\n        2\n       </sub>\n       in Cassidy\'s suit during EVA 3 was attributed to the astronaut working at a fast pace.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd10_activities1_73-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd10_activities1-73">\n         [NASA 21]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd10_activities2_74-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd10_activities2-74">\n         [53]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd10_activities3_75-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd10_activities3-75">\n         [54]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="25_July_(Flight_Day_11)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="25_July_.28Flight_Day_11.29">\n        25 July (Flight Day 11)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: 25 July (Flight Day 11)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The crew of both the shuttle and station had a day off. The day was uneventful except for the station\'s American CO\n       <sub>\n        2\n       </sub>\n       removal system shutting down without any immediate impact.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd11_activities1_76-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd11_activities1-76">\n         [NASA 22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd11_activities2_77-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd11_activities2-77">\n         [55]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd11_activities3_78-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd11_activities3-78">\n         [56]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="26_July_(Flight_Day_12)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="26_July_.28Flight_Day_12.29">\n        26 July (Flight Day 12)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: 26 July (Flight Day 12)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The Japanese Exposed Section cargo carrier was berthed in Endeavour\xe2\x80\x99s payload bay by the shuttle\'s robotic arm after it was handed the pallet by the station\'s robotic arm. After this the crew of both the station and the shuttle held a joint news conference. Meanwhile, the malfunctioning American CO\n       <sub>\n        2\n       </sub>\n       removal system has been transitioned to manual mode in order to keep it running.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd12_activities1_79-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd12_activities1-79">\n         [NASA 23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd12_activities2_80-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd12_activities2-80">\n         [57]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd12_co2_81-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd12_co2-81">\n         [58]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="27_July_(Flight_Day_13,_EVA_5)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="27_July_.28Flight_Day_13.2C_EVA_5.29">\n        27 July (Flight Day 13, EVA 5)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: 27 July (Flight Day 13, EVA 5)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Astronauts_Tom_Marshburn_and_Christopher_Cassidy_STS-127_Space_walk_5.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/17/Astronauts_Tom_Marshburn_and_Christopher_Cassidy_STS-127_Space_walk_5.jpg/220px-Astronauts_Tom_Marshburn_and_Christopher_Cassidy_STS-127_Space_walk_5.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/17/Astronauts_Tom_Marshburn_and_Christopher_Cassidy_STS-127_Space_walk_5.jpg/330px-Astronauts_Tom_Marshburn_and_Christopher_Cassidy_STS-127_Space_walk_5.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/17/Astronauts_Tom_Marshburn_and_Christopher_Cassidy_STS-127_Space_walk_5.jpg/440px-Astronauts_Tom_Marshburn_and_Christopher_Cassidy_STS-127_Space_walk_5.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Astronauts_Tom_Marshburn_and_Christopher_Cassidy_STS-127_Space_walk_5.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Marshburn and Cassidy during space walk 5.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Cassidy and Marshburn started EVA 5 at 11:33 UTC when they switched their suit power to internal battery. For this spacewalk, the CO\n       <sub>\n        2\n       </sub>\n       absorbent system in the suits were changed from\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lithium_Hydroxide" title="Lithium Hydroxide">\n        Lithium Hydroxide\n       </a>\n       to METOX due to problems with Cassidy\'s usage. Cassidy completed the reconfiguring of power channels in the Zenith 1 patch panel which are used for the control moment gyroscopes. Before the rewiring, two of the gyroscopes were fed by the same power channel. Since a failure of the channel can knock down two gyros and put the station in a degraded position the reconfiguration was made necessary. This rewiring made the two gyros to operate from separate power channels. Meanwhile, Marshburn secured some multi-layered insulation on the Dextre. Later both the spacewalkers installed video cameras on the front and back of the Japanese exposed facility which will be used in dockings of the Japanese cargo crafts and normal operation. The cameras flew up in launch configuration and now have been installed in an operational configuration, thus completing the JEF assembly. Meanwhile, due to Cassidy\'s METOX limitation, the deployment of the PAS was deferred to a future spacewalk. Instead some get ahead tasks were completed which included installation of handrails and a portable foot restraint.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd13_activities1_82-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd13_activities1-82">\n         [NASA 24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd13_plan_83-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd13_plan-83">\n         [59]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd13_activities2_84-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd13_activities2-84">\n         [60]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd13_activities3_85-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd13_activities3-85">\n         [61]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd13_activities4_86-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd13_activities4-86">\n         [62]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="28_July_(Flight_Day_14,_ISS_Undocking)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="28_July_.28Flight_Day_14.2C_ISS_Undocking.29">\n        28 July (Flight Day 14, ISS Undocking)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: 28 July (Flight Day 14, ISS Undocking)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       After a crew farewell Endeavour undocked from the ISS at 17:26 UTC. Unlike most other launches, hatch closure, which happened at 15:08 UTC, and undocking happened on the same day due to the extended delay in launching and the arrival of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Progress_M-67" title="Progress M-67">\n        Progress 34\n       </a>\n       cargo craft. After undocking Hurley began a fly around of the station giving the shuttle crew an opportunity to photograph the station\'s current configuration in all directions. Then a final separation burn was completed at 3:09\xc2\xa0pm EDT.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd14_activities1_87-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd14_activities1-87">\n         [NASA 25]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd14_activities2_88-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd14_activities2-88">\n         [63]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd14_activities3_89-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd14_activities3-89">\n         [64]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Endeavour_shortly_after_shuttle_and_station_post-undocking_separation.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2843" data-file-width="4282" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e7/Endeavour_shortly_after_shuttle_and_station_post-undocking_separation.jpg/120px-Endeavour_shortly_after_shuttle_and_station_post-undocking_separation.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e7/Endeavour_shortly_after_shuttle_and_station_post-undocking_separation.jpg/180px-Endeavour_shortly_after_shuttle_and_station_post-undocking_separation.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e7/Endeavour_shortly_after_shuttle_and_station_post-undocking_separation.jpg/240px-Endeavour_shortly_after_shuttle_and_station_post-undocking_separation.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Endeavour shortly after the shuttle and station post-undocking separation.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35.5px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:ISS_%26_Endeavour_Shadow_STS-127_2.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2828" data-file-width="4288" height="79" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ed/ISS_%26_Endeavour_Shadow_STS-127_2.jpg/120px-ISS_%26_Endeavour_Shadow_STS-127_2.jpg" </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           ISS shortly after the shuttle and station post-undocking separation with the JEF prominently seen.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="29_July_(Flight_Day_15)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="29_July_.28Flight_Day_15.29">\n        29 July (Flight Day 15)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: 29 July (Flight Day 15)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Layers_of_Earth%27s_atmosphere,_brightly_colored_as_the_sun_sets.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Layers_of_Earth%27s_atmosphere%2C_brightly_colored_as_the_sun_sets.jpg/220px-Layers_of_Earth%27s_atmosphere%2C_brightly_colored_as_the_sun_sets.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Layers_of_Earth%27s_atmosphere%2C_brightly_colored_as_the_sun_sets.jpg/330px-Layers_of_Earth%27s_atmosphere%2C_brightly_colored_as_the_sun_sets.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Layers_of_Earth%27s_atmosphere%2C_brightly_colored_as_the_sun_sets.jpg/440px-Layers_of_Earth%27s_atmosphere%2C_brightly_colored_as_the_sun_sets.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Layers_of_Earth%27s_atmosphere,_brightly_colored_as_the_sun_sets.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Image of orbital sunset taken from Endeavour one day before the shuttle landed.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The OBSS was grappled by the shuttle\'s robotic arm and used to inspect Endeavour\xe2\x80\x99s thermal protection system for damage from orbital debris. The imagery will be analyzed to clear the shuttle for reentry.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd15_activities1_90-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd15_activities1-90">\n         [NASA 26]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Meanwhile, the foam loss on the external tank was initially attributed to substrate contamination ahead of the application of the foam.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-et131_foamloss_91-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-et131_foamloss-91">\n         [65]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Later during the processing of\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-128" title="STS-128">\n        STS-128\n       </a>\n       , voids in the foam was highlighted as a trigger for the shedding. The air trapped in the voids could have expanded due to the high temperatures generated during ascent thus breaking the foam.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-et132_foam1_92-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-et132_foam1-92">\n         [66]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-et132_foam_93-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-et132_foam-93">\n         [67]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="30_July_(Flight_Day_16)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="30_July_.28Flight_Day_16.29">\n        30 July (Flight Day 16)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: 30 July (Flight Day 16)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The crew checked out the shuttle\'s systems for the landing, and successfully deployed the\n       <a href="/wiki/DRAGONSat" title="DRAGONSat">\n        DRAGONSat\n       </a>\n       and ANDE-2 satellites. The shuttle was cleared for reentry, with the TPS imagery showing no concerns.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd16_activities1_94-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd16_activities1-94">\n         [NASA 27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd16_activities2_95-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd16_activities2-95">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-96">\n        <a href="#cite_note-96">\n         [69]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The shuttle tracked two chances of landing at KSC on 31 July, and could land no later due to its limited\n       <a href="/wiki/Carbon_dioxide" title="Carbon dioxide">\n        carbon dioxide\n       </a>\n       -scrubbing LiOH supply.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd16_activities3_97-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd16_activities3-97">\n         [70]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="31_July_(Flight_Day_17,_Landing)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="31_July_.28Flight_Day_17.2C_Landing.29">\n        31 July (Flight Day 17, Landing)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: 31 July (Flight Day 17, Landing)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       After a 16-day mission,\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       landed successfully at Kennedy Space Center at 10:48 EDT on 31 July 2009. The landing had to be undertaken before 1 August, due to CO\n       <sub>\n        2\n       </sub>\n       -scrubbing\n       <a href="/wiki/Lithium_hydroxide" title="Lithium hydroxide">\n        lithium hydroxide\n       </a>\n       limitations. There were two opportunities to land on 31 July, of which the first was ultimately utilized.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd17_landing1_98-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd17_landing1-98">\n         [NASA 28]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fd17_landing2_99-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fd17_landing2-99">\n         [71]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-127_Landing_02.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="1993" data-file-width="3000" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/STS-127_Landing_02.jpg/120px-STS-127_Landing_02.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/STS-127_Landing_02.jpg/180px-STS-127_Landing_02.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/STS-127_Landing_02.jpg/240px-STS-127_Landing_02.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <i>\n            Endeavour\n           </i>\n           touches down at Kennedy Space Center.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-127_Landing_01.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2008" data-file-width="3000" height="80" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/STS-127_Landing_01.jpg/180px-STS-127_Landing_01.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/STS-127_Landing_01.jpg/240px-STS-127_Landing_01.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <i>\n            Endeavour\n           </i>\n           deploys its drag chute to aid deceleration.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="EVAs">\n        EVAs\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: EVAs">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       Five\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Extra-vehicular_activity" title="Extra-vehicular activity">\n        spacewalks\n       </a>\n       were conducted during STS-127.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-presskit_4-10">\n        <a href="#cite_note-presskit-4">\n         [NASA 1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable">\n       <tr>\n        <th style="width:5em;">\n         EVA\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Spacewalkers\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Start (\n         <a href="/wiki/Coordinated_Universal_Time" title="Coordinated Universal Time">\n          UTC\n         </a>\n         )\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         End (UTC)\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Duration\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td rowspan="2">\n         EVA 1\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/David_Wolf_(astronaut)" title="David Wolf (astronaut)">\n          David A. Wolf\n         </a>\n         <br/>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Timothy_L._Kopra" title="Timothy L.        Wake-up calls\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-127&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Wake-up calls">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       NASA began a tradition of playing music to astronauts during the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gemini_program" title="Gemini program">\n        Gemini program\n       </a>\n       , and first used music to wake up a flight crew during\n       <a href="/wiki/Apollo_15" title="Apollo 15">\n        Apollo 15\n       </a>\n       . Each track is specially chosen, often by the astronauts\' families, and usually has a special meaning to an individual member of the crew, or is applicable to their daily activities.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-chronology_101-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-chronology-101">\n         [NASA 30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wakeup_102-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wakeup-102">\n         [NASA 31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable">\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n
